(********************************************************************

 The Kleisli category

 The usual definition of the Kleisli category (given in the file
 `Monads.KleisliCategory.v` does not give rise to a univalent
 category. In this file, we give an alternative definition of the
 Kleisli category in such a way that we do get a univalent category.
 This definition can be found here:

 https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/Kleisli+category#in_terms_of_free_algebras

 We also prove its universal property.

 Note: to prove its universal property, we use that the usual
 definition of the Kleisli category (which is not necessarily
 univalent), satisfies the universal property. We also use that we
 have a weak equivalence between these two categories.

 Contents
 1. The free algebra functor
 2. The univalent Kleisli category
 3. The weak equivalence
 4. The universal property

 ********************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]
Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.
[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

(**
 1. The free algebra functor
 *)
Section FreeAlgebraFunctor.
  Context {C : category}
          (m : Monad C).

  
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_data C (eilenberg_moore_cat m)

  
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_data C (eilenberg_moore_cat m)

    
C: category
m: Monad C
C → eilenberg_moore_cat m
C: category
m: Monad C
∏ a b : C,
C ⟦ a, b ⟧ → eilenberg_moore_cat m ⟦ ?F a, ?F b ⟧

    
C: category
m: Monad C
C → eilenberg_moore_cat m
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
η m (m x) · μ m x = identity (m x)
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
μ m (m x) · μ m x = # m (μ m x) · μ m x

      
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
η m (m x) · μ m x = identity (m x)
 apply Monad_law1.
      
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
μ m (m x) · μ m x = # m (μ m x) · μ m x
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
# m (μ m x) · μ m x = μ m (m x) · μ m x

        apply Monad_law3.
    
C: category
m: Monad C
∏ a b : C,
C ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ eilenberg_moore_cat m
  ⟦ (λ x : C,
     make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
       (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x)) a,
  (λ x : C,
   make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
     (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x)) b ⟧
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
C
⟦ pr11 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
          (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x)),
pr11 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m y) (μ m y)
        (Monad_law1 y) (! Monad_law3 y)) ⟧
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr21 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
        (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x)) · ?f =
# m ?f
· pr21 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m y) (μ m y)
          (Monad_law1 y) (! Monad_law3 y))

      
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
C
⟦ pr11 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
          (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x)),
pr11 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m y) (μ m y)
        (Monad_law1 y) (! Monad_law3 y)) ⟧
 exact (#m f).
      
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr21 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
        (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x)) · # m f =
# m (# m f)
· pr21 (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m y) (μ m y)
          (Monad_law1 y) (! Monad_law3 y))
 exact (!(nat_trans_ax (μ m) _ _ f)).
  Defined.

  
C: category
m: Monad C
is_functor free_alg_em_data

  
C: category
m: Monad C
is_functor free_alg_em_data

    
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_idax free_alg_em_data
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_compax free_alg_em_data

    
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_idax free_alg_em_data
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
# free_alg_em_data (identity x) =
identity (free_alg_em_data x)

      
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
# m (identity x) = identity (m x)

      apply functor_id.
    
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_compax free_alg_em_data
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
# free_alg_em_data (f · g) =
# free_alg_em_data f · # free_alg_em_data g

      
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
# m (f · g) = # m f · # m g

      apply functor_comp.
  Qed.

  
C: category
m: Monad C
C ⟶ eilenberg_moore_cat m

  
C: category
m: Monad C
C ⟶ eilenberg_moore_cat m

    
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_data C (eilenberg_moore_cat m)
C: category
m: Monad C
is_functor ?F

    
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_data C (eilenberg_moore_cat m)
 exact free_alg_em_data.
    
C: category
m: Monad C
is_functor free_alg_em_data
 exact free_alg_em_is_functor.
  Defined.
End FreeAlgebraFunctor.

(**
 2. The univalent Kleisli category
 *)
Definition kleisli_cat
           {C : category}
           (m : Monad C)
  : category
  := full_img_sub_precategory (free_alg_em m).

Definition univalent_kleisli_cat
           {C : univalent_category}
           (m : Monad C)
  : univalent_category
  := @univalent_image
       C
       (eilenberg_moore_univalent_cat C m)
       (free_alg_em m).


C: category
m: Monad C
x₁, x₂: kleisli_cat m
f: kleisli_cat m ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism (pr111 f)
is_z_isomorphism f


C: category
m: Monad C
x₁, x₂: kleisli_cat m
f: kleisli_cat m ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism (pr111 f)
is_z_isomorphism f

  
C: category
m: Monad C
x₁, x₂: kleisli_cat m
f: kleisli_cat m ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism (pr111 f)
is_z_isomorphism (pr1 f)

  
C: category
m: Monad C
x₁, x₂: kleisli_cat m

is_z_isomorphism (pr111 f)

  exact Hf.
Defined.

 exact (maponpaths (λ z, pr111 z) (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso f)).
    
C: category

f: z_iso x₁ x₂
pr111 (inv_from_z_iso f) · pr111 (pr1 f) =
identity (pr111 x₂)
 exact (maponpaths (λ z, pr111 z) (z_iso_after_z_iso_inv f)).
Defined.

Definition kleisli_incl
           {C : category}
           (m : Monad C)
  : C ⟶ kleisli_cat m
  := functor_full_img _.


C: category
m: Monad C
m ∙ kleisli_incl m ⟹ kleisli_incl m


C: category
m: Monad C
m ∙ kleisli_incl m ⟹ kleisli_incl m

  
C: category
m: Monad C
nat_trans_data (m ∙ kleisli_incl m) (kleisli_incl m)
C: category
m: Monad C
is_nat_trans (m ∙ kleisli_incl m) (kleisli_incl m) ?t

  
C: category
m: Monad C
nat_trans_data (m ∙ kleisli_incl m) (kleisli_incl m)
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
kleisli_cat m ⟦ (m ∙ kleisli_incl m) x,
kleisli_incl m x ⟧

    
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
eilenberg_moore_cat m ⟦ (m ∙ kleisli_incl m) x,
kleisli_incl m x ⟧

    
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
C ⟦ m (m x), m x ⟧
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
μ m (m x) · ?Goal = # m ?Goal · μ m x

    
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
C ⟦ m (m x), m x ⟧
 exact (μ m x).
    
C: category
m: Monad C
x: C
μ m (m x) · μ m x = # m (μ m x) · μ m x
 abstract
        (refine (!_) ;
         apply Monad_law3).
  
C: category
m: Monad C
is_nat_trans (m ∙ kleisli_incl m) (kleisli_incl m)
  ((λ x : C,
    make_mor_eilenberg_moore m
      (μ m x
       :
       C ⟦ pr11 ((m ∙ kleisli_incl m) x),
       pr11 (kleisli_incl m x) ⟧)
      (kleisli_nat_trans_subproof C m x
       :
       pr21 ((m ∙ kleisli_incl m) x)
       · (μ m x
          :
          C ⟦ pr11 ((m ∙ kleisli_incl m) x),
          pr11 (kleisli_incl m x) ⟧) =
       # m
         (μ m x
          :
          C ⟦ pr11 ((m ∙ kleisli_incl m) x),
          pr11 (kleisli_incl m x) ⟧)
       · pr21 (kleisli_incl m x)),, tt)
   :
   nat_trans_data (m ∙ kleisli_incl m)
     (kleisli_incl m))
 abstract
      (intros x y f ;
       use eq_mor_kleisli_cat ; cbn ;
       apply (nat_trans_ax (μ m))).
Defined.

(**
 3. The weak equivalence
 *)

C: category
m: Monad C
functor_data (Kleisli_cat_monad m) (kleisli_cat m)


C: category
m: Monad C
functor_data (Kleisli_cat_monad m) (kleisli_cat m)

  
C: category
m: Monad C
Kleisli_cat_monad m → kleisli_cat m
C: category
m: Monad C
∏ a b : Kleisli_cat_monad m,
Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ kleisli_cat m ⟦ ?F a, ?F b ⟧

  
C: category
m: Monad C
Kleisli_cat_monad m → kleisli_cat m
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x: Kleisli_cat_monad m
z_iso (free_alg_em m x) (free_alg_em m x)

    apply identity_z_iso.
  
C: category
m: Monad C
∏ a b : Kleisli_cat_monad m,
Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ kleisli_cat m
  ⟦ (λ x : Kleisli_cat_monad m,
     free_alg_em m x,,
     hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x))) a,
  (λ x : Kleisli_cat_monad m,
   free_alg_em m x,,
   hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x))) b ⟧
 
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad m
f: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ x, y ⟧
eilenberg_moore_cat m
⟦ free_alg_em m x,,
  hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x)),
free_alg_em m y,,
hinhpr (y,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m y)) ⟧

    
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad m
f: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ x, y ⟧
C
⟦ pr11 (free_alg_em m x,,
        hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x))),
pr11 (free_alg_em m y,,
      hinhpr (y,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m y))) ⟧
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad m
f: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr21 (free_alg_em m x,,
      hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x)))
· ?f =
# m ?f
· pr21 (free_alg_em m y,,
        hinhpr (y,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m y)))

    
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad m
f: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ x, y ⟧
C
⟦ pr11 (free_alg_em m x,,
        hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x))),
pr11 (free_alg_em m y,,
      hinhpr (y,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m y))) ⟧
 exact (# m f · μ m y).
    
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad m
f: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr21 (free_alg_em m x,,
      hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x)))
· (# m f · μ m y) =
# m (# m f · μ m y)
· pr21 (free_alg_em m y,,
        hinhpr (y,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m y)))
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         rewrite !assoc ;
         refine (maponpaths (λ z, z · _) (!(nat_trans_ax (μ m) _ _ f)) @ _) ;
         cbn ;
         rewrite !functor_comp ;
         rewrite !assoc' ;
         apply maponpaths ;
         refine (!_) ;
         apply Monad_law3).
Defined.

C: category

# m (η m x) · μ m x = identity (m x)

    apply Monad_law2.
  
C: category
m: Monad C
functor_compax (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data m)
 
C: category
m: Monad C

f: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ y, z ⟧
# (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data m) (f · g) =
# (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data m) f
· # (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data m) g

    
C: category

x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad m

g: Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ y, z ⟧
pr111 (# (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data m) (f · g)) =
pr111 (# (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data m) f
       · # (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data m) g)

    
C: category

     (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C m x y
        (pr1 ψ₁)),, tt) =
(λ z : ∑
       x0 : eilenberg_moore_cat m
            ⟦ make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x)
                (μ m x) (Monad_law1 x)
                (! Monad_law3 x),
            make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m y)
              (μ m y) (Monad_law1 y)
              (! Monad_law3 y) ⟧,
       sub_precategory_predicate_morphisms
         (full_img_sub_precategory (free_alg_em m))
         (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
            (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x))
         (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m y) (μ m y)
            (Monad_law1 y) (! Monad_law3 y)) x0,
 η m x · pr111 z)
  (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m
     (# m (pr1 ψ₂) · μ m y)
     (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C m x y
        (pr1 ψ₂)),, tt)
pr1 ψ₁ = pr1 ψ₂

functor_to_kleisli_cat m y ⟧
ψ₁, ψ₂: hfiber
  (λ f : Kleisli_cat_monad m ⟦ x, y ⟧,
   # (functor_to_kleisli_cat m) f) f
p:= pr2 ψ₁ @ ! pr2 ψ₂: make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (# m (pr1 ψ₁) · μ m y)
  (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C m x y
     (pr1 ψ₁)),, tt =
make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (# m (pr1 ψ₂) · μ m y)
  (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C m x y
     (pr1 ψ₂)),, tt
q:= maponpaths
  (λ z : ∑
         _ : sub_precategory_morphisms
               (full_sub_precategory
                  (eilenberg_moore_cat_pred m))
               (m x,, μ m x) (m y,, μ m y), unit,
   η m x · pr111 z) p: η m x · (# m (pr1 ψ₁) · μ m y) =
η m x · (# m (pr1 ψ₂) · μ m y)
pr1 ψ₁ = pr1 ψ₂

      exact (!(nat_trans_ax (η m) _ _ (pr1 ψ₂))).

(**
 4. The universal property
 *)
Section KleisliUMP1.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : univalent_category}
          (m : Monad C₁)
          (F : C₁ ⟶ C₂)
          (γ : m ∙ F ⟹ F)
          (p₁ : ∏ (x : C₁), #F (η m x) · γ x = identity _)
          (p₂ : ∏ (x : C₁), γ _ · γ x = #F (μ m x) · γ x).

  Definition functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat
    : kleisli_cat m ⟶ C₂
    := lift_functor_along
         C₂
         (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (essentially_surjective_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (fully_faithful_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad m F γ p₁ p₂).

  Definition functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_nat_trans
    : kleisli_incl m ∙ functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat ⟹ F
    := nat_trans_comp
         _ _ _
         (nat_trans_comp
            _ _ _
            (post_whisker
               (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_z_iso m)
               functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat)
            (pre_whisker
               _
               (lift_functor_along_comm
                  C₂
                  (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
                  (essentially_surjective_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
                  (fully_faithful_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
                  (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad m F γ p₁ p₂))))
         (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad_nat_trans m F γ p₁ p₂).

  
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
m: Monad C₁
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
γ: m ∙ F ⟹ F
p₁: ∏ x : C₁,
# F (η m x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C₁ x))
p₂: ∏ x : C₁, γ (m x) · γ x = # F (μ m x) · γ x
is_nat_z_iso
  functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_nat_trans

  
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
m: Monad C₁
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
γ: m ∙ F ⟹ F
p₁: ∏ x : C₁,
# F (η m x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C₁ x))
p₂: ∏ x : C₁, γ (m x) · γ x = # F (μ m x) · γ x
is_nat_z_iso
  functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_nat_trans

    
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
m: Monad C₁
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
γ: m ∙ F ⟹ F
p₁: ∏ x : C₁,
# F (η m x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C₁ x))
p₂: ∏ x : C₁, γ (m x) · γ x = # F (μ m x) · γ x
is_nat_z_iso
  (nat_trans_comp
     (functor_composite_data (kleisli_incl m)
        functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat)
     (functor_composite_data (Left_Kleisli_functor m)
        (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad m F γ p₁ p₂))
     F
     (nat_trans_comp
        (functor_composite_data (kleisli_incl m)
           functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat)
        (functor_composite_data
           (Left_Kleisli_functor m
            ∙ functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
           functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat)
        (functor_composite_data
           (Left_Kleisli_functor m)
           (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad m F γ p₁ p₂))
        (post_whisker
           (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_z_iso m)
           functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat)
        (pre_whisker (Left_Kleisli_functor m)
           (lift_functor_along_comm C₂
              (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
              (essentially_surjective_functor_to_kleisli_cat
                 m)
              (fully_faithful_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
              (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad m F γ p₁
                 p₂))))
     (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad_nat_trans m F γ
        p₁ p₂))

Section KleisliUMP2.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : univalent_category}
          (m : Monad C₁)
          {G₁ G₂ : kleisli_cat m ⟶ C₂}
          (α : kleisli_incl m ∙ G₁ ⟹ kleisli_incl m ∙ G₂)
          (p : ∏ (x : C₁),
               #G₁ (kleisli_nat_trans m x) · α x
               =
               α (m x) · # G₂ (kleisli_nat_trans m x)).

  Definition nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help
    : Left_Kleisli_functor m ∙ (functor_to_kleisli_cat m ∙ G₁)
      ⟹
      Left_Kleisli_functor m ∙ (functor_to_kleisli_cat m ∙ G₂)
    := nat_trans_comp
         _ _ _
         (nat_trans_comp
            _ _ _
            (post_whisker
               (nat_z_iso_inv (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_z_iso m))
               _)
            α)
         (post_whisker
            (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_z_iso m)
            _).

  
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
m: Monad C₁
G₁, G₂: kleisli_cat m ⟶ C₂
α: kleisli_incl m ∙ G₁ ⟹ kleisli_incl m ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,
# G₁ (kleisli_nat_trans m x) · α x =
α (m x) · # G₂ (kleisli_nat_trans m x)
x: C₁
# (functor_to_kleisli_cat m ∙ G₁)
  (kleisli_monad_nat_trans m x)
· nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help x =
nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help (m x)
· # (functor_to_kleisli_cat m ∙ G₂)
    (kleisli_monad_nat_trans m x)

m: Monad C₁

C₁, C₂: univalent_category
m: Monad C₁
G₁, G₂: kleisli_cat m ⟶ C₂
α: kleisli_incl m ∙ G₁ ⟹ kleisli_incl m ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,

· # G₂
    (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (μ m x)
       (kleisli_nat_trans_subproof C₁ m x),, tt) =
# (pr1 G₁)
  (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (identity (m (m x)))
     (pr1
        (Dialgebras.is_z_iso_disp_dialgebra m
           (functor_identity C₁)
           (is_z_isomorphism_identity (m (m x)))
           (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_trans_subproof
              C₁ m (m x)))),, tt) · α (m x)
· # (pr1 G₂)
    (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (identity (m (m x)))
       (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_trans_subproof
          C₁ m (m x)),, tt)
· # G₂
    (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m
       (# m (identity (m x)) · μ m x)
       (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C₁ m
          (m x) x (identity (m x))),, tt)

m: Monad C₁

· # G₂
    (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (μ m x)
       (kleisli_nat_trans_subproof C₁ m x),, tt) =
# (pr1 G₁)
  (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (identity (m (m x)))
     (pr1
        (Dialgebras.is_z_iso_disp_dialgebra m
           (functor_identity C₁)
           (is_z_isomorphism_identity (m (m x)))
           (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_trans_subproof
              C₁ m (m x)))),, tt)
· (α (m x)
   · (# (pr1 G₂)
        (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m
           (identity (m (m x)))
           (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_trans_subproof
              C₁ m (m x)),, tt)
      · # G₂
          (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m
             (# m (identity (m x)) · μ m x)
             (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C₁
                m (m x) x (identity (m x))),, tt)))

  Definition nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat
    : G₁ ⟹ G₂
    := lift_nat_trans_along
         C₂
         (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (essentially_surjective_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (fully_faithful_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (nat_trans_from_kleisli_cat_monad
            m
            nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help
            nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help_eq).

p: ∏ x : C₁,
# G₁ (kleisli_nat_trans m x) · α x =
α (m x) · # G₂ (kleisli_nat_trans m x)
pre_whisker (kleisli_incl m)
  nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat = α

  (lift_nat_trans_along_comm C₂
     (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)

        nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help_eq))

  nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help
  nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help_eq x

    (make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (identity (m x))

          C₁ m x),, tt)

m: Monad C₁

        apply idpath.
      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
m: Monad C₁
G₁, G₂: kleisli_cat m ⟶ C₂
α: kleisli_incl m ∙ G₁ ⟹ kleisli_incl m ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,
# G₁ (kleisli_nat_trans m x) · α x =

β₁, β₂: G₁ ⟹ G₂
q₁: pre_whisker (kleisli_incl m) β₁ = α
q₂: pre_whisker (kleisli_incl m) β₂ = α
x: C₁
identity
  (G₁
     (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
        (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x),,
      hinhpr
        (x,,
         identity_z_iso
           (make_ob_eilenberg_moore m (m x) (μ m x)
              (Monad_law1 x) (! Monad_law3 x)))))
· α x = α x

      apply id_left.
  Qed.
